[30;1m34 | [0m[35m    Returns list of utf-8 byte and a corresponding list of unicode strings.[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35m    The reversible bpe codes work on unicode strings.[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35m    This means you need a large # of unicode characters in your vocab if you want to avoid UNKs.[0m

[30;1m39 | [0m[35m    To avoid that, we want lookup tables between utf-8 bytes and unicode strings.[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35m    And avoids mapping to whitespace/control characters the bpe code barfs on.[0m
